| OPP-0002192442 | DCG | 1. Matrix Computation Performance - (Checks Silicon Integrity & Peak Throughput; Thermal & Power Stability (Sustained Performance; Driver & Firmware Optimization; Software Stack Efficiency (cuBLAS))<br> <br>Matrix computation performance shall be tested in accordance with NVIDIA’s official Benchmark Step-by-Step Guide for B200/GB200, using PeakTOPS measurements and cublasMatmulBench to evaluate sustained matrix multiplication (MatMul) throughput. The GPUs shall be deemed compliant only if measured performance achieves not less than ninety-five percent (95%) of NVIDIA-published or NVIDIA-validated reference performance under equivalent test conditions.<br><br>2. Inter-GPU Communication Performance - ( Validates The "East-West" Network (The Fabric); Intra-Node and Inter-Node Topology; NCCL Library Efficiency - bandwidth & latency)<br> <br>Inter-GPU and interconnect communication performance shall be evaluated using NVIDIA NCCL Tests, executed from the official repository at https://github.com/NVIDIA/nccl-tests. Metrics including bandwidth and latency shall be measured across the applicable GPU topology. Acceptance shall require measured results to achieve not less than ninety-five percent (95%) of NVIDIA reference performance for the same configuration.<br> <br>3. Model Training Efficiency<br> <br>Model efficiency and end-to-end training performance shall be evaluated using Megatron with open-source tooling to conduct training runs of the Llama 3 – 70B model. Training throughput metrics, including tokens per second and step time, shall meet not less than ninety-five percent (95%) of NVIDIA-validated or widely recognized open-source reference benchmarks for NVIDIA B200/GB200 under equivalent conditions. |
